solempnite solempnite done euery kyng toke wif lad hem owne cōtre ther made hem quenes befell thus afterward y• dame albyne bicome stoute sterne tolde litel pris lorde hym scorne despit wolde done wolde haue hir owne diuerse mater hir othir sustres e • ichone hem euel ayenst hir lordes wonder wyt moch hem thought hir husbondes nought hie • age comē hir fadre tho kynges hir lordis wolde haue chastized hem fair speche behestes also yeftes warned hem fair maner vpon loue frendshipp sholde amende l • ther condicions nought didden owne wyll thyng hem liked poer wherfor tho xxxiij kynges vpon dioclisian saw herd many playntes doughtres sore aschamed become wonder angrie wroth toward hi • doughtres thought nyght day yf tho myght amend y• mysded anone sent lr̄ez vn xxxiij kynges shold come hym bring hem hir wife euerichone certain day wolde ther chastise wikkednesse yf myght maner wyse y• kynges comē day tyme tho sette bitwene hem kyng dioclisian hem vnderfeng moche honour made solempne fest vnder lordshipp thridde day solempnite kyng dioclisian sent xxxiij doughtres shold come speke hym chambre come spake vn hem hir wikkednesse hir cruelte dispitously hem reproued vndernam toke hym grete damage lande left home behynd hym man kepe lande nōme hem hym fro lande xxxm knyghtes doughty mēnys body went ouer lande amorican ther slewe kyng called imball conqnered lande done
